 function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
     var d = new Date();
     d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
     var expires = "expires=" + d.toGMTString();
     document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
 }
 
 function getCookie(cname) {
     var name = cname + "=";
     var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
     for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
             c = c.substring(1);
         }
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
             return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
         }
     }
     return "";
 }
 
 function clean_string(q) {
     /* this will clean the query for any invalid encodings */
     /* this can be used for the filter values also */
 
     if (q) {
             q = q.replace(/\+/g, " ");
        		 q = q.replace(/\*/g, "");
 //         return decodeURI(q);
 
       try{
 	     return decodeURIComponent(decodeURIComponent(q))
 
       }catch (e){
     	return q;
       }
 
 
     } else {
         return q;
     }
 }
 function get_keyword() {
     try {
         var q = window.location.search.split('q=')[1].split("&")[0];
     } catch (e) {
         var q = '';
     }
     return clean_string(q);
 }
 
 function get_rly_keyword() {
     try {
         var rly_keyword = window.location.search.split('rly_keyword=')[1].split("&")[0];
     } catch (e) {
         var rly_keyword = '';
     }
     return clean_string(rly_keyword);
 }
 
 
   function get_variant_id(){
         try {
         var vid = window.location.search.split('variant=')[1].split("&")[0];
     } catch (e) {
         var vid = '';
     }
     return clean_string(vid);
   }
    function get_product_id(){
         try {
         var pid = window.location.search.split('rly_pid=')[1].split("&")[0];
     } catch (e) {
         var pid = '';
     }
     return clean_string(pid);
   }
 
   function get_rly_click_type() {
     try {
         var rly_click_type = window.location.search.split('rly_referral_type=')[1].split("&")[0];
     } catch (e) {
         var rly_click_type = '';
     }
     return clean_string(rly_click_type);
 }
 
 
   function get_rly_click_type_from_text(text) {
     try {
         var rly_click_type = text.split('rly_referral_type=')[1].split("&")[0];
     } catch (e) {
         var rly_click_type = '';
     }
     return clean_string(rly_click_type);
 }
   function generateUniqueId() {
     var text = "";
     var possible = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789";
 
     for (var i = 0; i < 10; i++)
       text += possible.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * possible.length));
     return text;
   }
 
 
     function get_or_create_relishly_track_id() {
         var tracker_cookie_name = 'relishly-shopify-' + store_name + '-tracking-id';
         var session_id = getCookie(tracker_cookie_name);
         if (session_id) {
             return session_id;
         } else {
             var session_id = generateUniqueId();
             setCookie(tracker_cookie_name, session_id, 365);
             return session_id;
         }
     }

       }
     });
 
 
 
     }

     $(document).on("click", ".product-card a, .product-autocomplete-card", function() {
         /*
         This is when the user searched a keyword and clicked some product card
 
         The css selectors we are using here are from our theme, so
         these things are not variable.
 
         //click_type can be ac or product_click
         */
       	search_keyword = get_keyword();
         data = {};
 //        a = new URL(location.href);
         event_data['keyword'] = $(this).attr('data-keyword');
 
         event_data['referral_type'] = $(this).attr('data-click-type');
 
       	url = window.location.origin + $(this).attr('href');
         event_data['url'] = url
 
 		// send handle, product_id, variant_id
 
 
         try{
           handle = $(this).attr('href').replace("/products/","");
           handle_cleaned = handle.split("?")[0];
           event_data['handle'] = handle_cleaned;
         }catch(e){
 
         }
        try{
          product_id = $(this).attr('href').split("rly_pid=")[1];
          if (product_id.indexOf('&') >= 0){
           	 product_id = product_id.split("&")[0];
          }
           event_data['product_id'] = product_id;
         }catch(e){
 			console.log(e);
         }
       try{
          variant_id = $(this).attr('href').split("variant=")[1];
          if (variant_id.indexOf('&') >= 0){
           	 variant_id = variant_id.split("&")[0];
          }
           event_data['variant_id'] = variant_id;
         }catch(e){
           			console.log(e);
 
 
         }
 
 
         data['event_data'] = event_data;
         data['event_type'] = "item_click";
         post_data(data, false);
 
 
     });

     $('button').click(function(event) {
         var btn_text = $(this).text();
 
  //   try {
  //           var search_keyword = window.location.href.split("utm_keyword=")[1];
  //       } catch (e) {
  //           search_keyword = null;
  //       }
 
 
         if (btn_text) {
             btn_text = btn_text.toLowerCase();
             if (btn_text.indexOf('cart') >= 0) {
               var product_variant_id = "";
               var product_id = "";
 
                try{
 
                   product_variant_id = $('input[name="id"]').val();
                   product_id = $($('.product-form--alt form')[0]).attr('data-productid')
 
 
                 }catch(e){
 
 
                 }
               event_data['variant_id'] = product_variant_id; // sku ?
               event_data['product_id'] = product_id;
               variant_id_from_url = get_variant_id();
               product_id_from_url = get_product_id();
 
               if(variant_id_from_url){
                 event_data['variant_id'] = variant_id_from_url;
               }
               if (product_id_from_url){
                 event_data['product_id'] = product_id_from_url;
 
               }
               handle = window.location.pathname.replace("/products/","");
               handle_cleaned = handle.split("?")[0];
               event_data['handle'] = handle_cleaned;
 
                 data['event_type'] = "cart_add";
                 event_data['keyword'] = get_rly_keyword();
 
               	event_data['referral_type'] = get_rly_click_type();
                 data['event_data'] = event_data;
                 post_data(data, true);
             }
         }
     });
 });

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function($) {
 
 
     SEARCH_PAGE_PATH = "/pages/search-page";
 
     if (is_autocomplete_enabled && is_theme_installed && is_relishly_key_verified) {
 
 
       $('input[name="q"]').each(function( index ) {
 
       input = $(this);
 //       console.log(input);
       input.off();// remove any listeners from the theme
 
       input.attr("action",SEARCH_PAGE_PATH);
       var form = $(input).parents('form:first');
       form.attr("action",SEARCH_PAGE_PATH);
 
 
       buttons = form.find('button[type="button"], button[type="submit"]')
 
       for(i=0;  i <buttons.length; i++){
         	btn = $(buttons[i])
          	btn.unbind(); // removing existing listerens on button/submit type
            					// of the autocomplete form.
         	btn.click(function(){
             var form = $(this).parents('form:first');
          		form.submit();
         	});
       }
 
       // SUGGESTION: find a way to clean the listeners on the input selector
       // may be wait for 500 ms to let all the listeners applied from the theme ?
 
 
 
 //       input = $(RELISHLY_AUTOCOMPLETE_SELECTOR)
 
 
       input.autocomplete({
             source: function(request, response) {
                 term = request.term;
                 var currentRequest = null;
 
                 currentRequest = $.ajax({
                     url: RELISHLY_AUTOCOMPLETE_API,
                     beforeSend: function() {
                         if (currentRequest != null) {
                             currentRequest.abort();
                         }
                     },
                     data: {
                         search_query: request.term,
                         api_token: apikey
 
                     },
                     response: function(event, ui) {
 
                     },
                     success: function(data) {
                         try {
                             var search_keyword_suggestions = data['search_queries'][0];
                         } catch (e) {
                             var search_keyword_suggestions = [];
                         }
                         try {
                             var products_list = data['products'].splice(0, 5);
                         } catch (e) {
                             var products_list = [];
                         }
                         var products = search_keyword_suggestions;
                         if (products_list.length > 0) {
                             products.push({
                                 'products': true
                             });
                         }
                         for (i in products_list) {
                           	var product = products_list[i];
                           	product['keyword'] = term;
                             products.push(product);
                         }
 
                         response(products);
 
                     }
                 });
             },
             minLength: 2,
 
         }).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function(ul, item) {
 
             if (item.no_results) {
                 var inner_html = '<div class="relishly-autocomplete-div"><div class=""><p class="no-result">' + item.no_results + '</p></div></div>';
             } else if (item.viewall) {
                 var inner_html = '<div class="relishly-autocomplete-div"><div class=""><p><a href="'+SEARCH_PAGE_PATH+'?q=' + item.keyword + '"> view all </a></p></div></div>';
             } else if (item.delimiter) {
                 var inner_html = '<div class="relishly-autocomplete-div"><div class=""><hr></div></div>';
             } else if (item.products) {
 
                 var inner_html = '<div class="relishly-autocomplete-div"><div class="products">Products</div></div>';
             } else if (item.title){
 
 
               url_arg = "";
               if (item.variant_id){
                 url_arg = "?variant=" +  item.variant_id;
               }
 
               if(url_arg.indexOf("?") > -1 ){
 
                 url_arg += '&rly_keyword=' + item.keyword + '&rly_referral_type=ac'+ '&rly_pid='+item.id ;
 
               }else{
                 url_arg += '?rly_keyword=' + item.keyword + '&rly_referral_type=ac'+ '&rly_pid='+item.id ;
 
               }
 
               var inner_html = '<a class="product-autocomplete-card" data-click-type="ac" data-keyword="'+item.keyword+'" href="/products/' + item.handle + url_arg +'" ><div class="relishly-autocomplete-div"><div class="image"><img src="' + item.image + '" ></div><div class="label"><h5>' + item.title + '</h5><p>' + item.price + '</p></div></div></a>';
             }else {
                 var inner_html = '<a href="'+SEARCH_PAGE_PATH+'?q=' + item.label + '" ><div class="relishly-autocomplete-div"><div class="relishly-keyword-suggestion"><p>' + item.label + '</p></div></a>';
 
             }
             return $("<li></li>")
                 .data("item.autocomplete", item)
                 .append(inner_html)
                 .appendTo(ul);
         };
 
         input.bind('autocompleteopen', function(event, data) {
             $('<li><a target="_blank" href="'+SEARCH_PAGE_PATH+'?q=' + +'">view all products</a></li>').appendTo('ul.ui-autocomplete');
 
             //       $('<li>Powered by <a target="_blank" href="http://relish.ai">relish.ai</a></li>').appendTo('ul.ui-autocomplete');
         });
 
 
       })
 
 
     };
 
 });
   </script>

  String.prototype.repeat = function(times) {
    times = parseInt(times);
    return (new Array(times + 1)).join(this);
 };
 
   function post_search_event(thedata, async) {
 
 
 
 
 
 
   $.ajax({
     type: "POST",
       url: RELISHLY_EVENTS_API + "?api_token=" + apikey,
       data: JSON.stringify(thedata),
     contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
     cache: false,
     async: async,
     success: function(data) {
       //console.log(data);
     },
     error: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown){
 //       console.log(errorThrown);
     }
   });
 
 
 
 
 
   }
 
   function track_search(search_keyword, filters_data, referer_url){
         // this will capture the keyword from url and sends to the event;
         var event_data = {};
         var thedata = {};
 
         if(filters_data.api_token){
           delete filters_data.api_token;
         }
         if(data.filters_data){
           delete filters_data.q;
         }
 
         event_data['url'] = referer_url;
         event_data['domain'] = window.location.hostname;
         event_data['keyword'] = get_keyword();
         event_data['keyword'] = get_keyword();
 
         event_data['filters'] = filters_data;
     	thedata['uid'] = get_or_create_relishly_track_id();
 
     	event_data['uid'] = get_or_create_relishly_track_id();
     	thedata['event_data'] = event_data;
 
 
         thedata['event_type'] = "search";
         post_search_event(thedata, true);
   }
 
 
     function detectmob() {
         if (navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i) ||
             navigator.userAgent.match(/webOS/i) ||
             navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) ||
             navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) ||
             navigator.userAgent.match(/iPod/i) ||
             navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i) ||
             navigator.userAgent.match(/Windows Phone/i)
         ) {
             return true;
         } else {
             return false;
         }
     }
 
 
 
 
     function change_url_state(labels) {
 //         var a = new URL(location.href);
 
         var new_url = window.location.search;
 
         for (i in labels) {
             new_url += "&" + labels[i].key + "=" + labels[i].value;
 
         }
 
         window.history.replaceState(null, null, new_url);
 
     }
 
     function listen_filters() {
         url_params = []
         $(RELISHLY_SEARCH_SIDEBAR).find('.fs-option.selected').each(function(i, el) {
             el = $(el);
 
             var d = {
                 'value': $(el).find('.fs-option-label').attr('data-value'),
                 'key': $(el).attr('data-group')
             }
             url_params.push(d);
         });
 
         q = get_keyword();
 
         var d = {
             'value': $('#relishly-sort-products').val(),
             'key': "sort_method"
         }
         url_params.push(d);
 
         change_url_state(url_params);
 
         get_search_results(q, 1, url_params); // get_page
 
     }
 
     function process_result_data(datas, search_query) {
         $("html, body").animate({
             scrollTop: 0
         }, "normal");
 
         var products_data = datas["products"]
         var filter_data = datas["filters"]
         $(RELISHLY_SEARCH_RESULTS).empty();
 
 
         var products_rendered_html_list = []
         $.each(products_data, function(index, data) {
             var product_card = render_product(data, search_query);
             products_rendered_html_list.push(product_card);
         });
         create_products_html(products_rendered_html_list);
         $(RELISHLY_SEARCH_RESULTS_PAGINATION).show();
 
 
         var filters_rendered_html_list = []
         $.each(filter_data, function(index, data) {
             var filter_card = render_filter(data);
             filters_rendered_html_list.push(filter_card);
         });
 
         create_filters_html(filters_rendered_html_list);
 
         $('.fs-option').click(function() {
             $el = $(this);
 
             if ($el.hasClass('selected')) {
                 $(this).removeClass('selected');
             } else {
                 $(this).addClass('selected');
             }
             listen_filters();
 //             $(".relishly-filters-slide-toggle").click();
 
         });
 
         $('.product-filter.fs-option').click(function() {
           	// just hide it,
           if ($('.relish-search-sidebar .box').css('display') == "block"){
              $(".relishly-filters-slide-toggle").click();
           }
 
 
 
         });
 
 
     }
 
     function render_pagination(page, totalPages, onclicked_call) {
         /* this will use bootstrap pagination lib to render the pagination */
 		/* onclicked_call will */
 
 
 
 
 //       console.log("currentpage is ", page, "; totalPages is :", totalPages);
 
 
 
       var $pagination = $(RELISHLY_SEARCH_RESULTS_PAGINATION);
       $pagination.html("");
 
       if(totalPages > 1){
 
 
 
         if(is_mobile){
       SHOW_MAX_PAGES = 2; // 2 shows 3 pages
 
         }else{
       SHOW_MAX_PAGES = 5; // 5 shows 6 pages
 
         }
 
       $pagination_elems = $('<ul class="pagination"></ul>');
 
 
 
       // check if there is prev button
       	// if prev ==  0, dont show to go beginning button
       // check if there is next button
       	// if next == totalPages dont show go to last
 
       pages_toshow = [];
       minPage = 1;
       maxPage = 5;
 
 //       pages_to_right_count = totalPages - page;
 //       pages_to_left_count = SHOW_MAX_PAGES - pages_to_right_count;
 
 //       if (pages_to_right_count >= SHOW_MAX_PAGES){
 
 
 //         console.log("pages_to_left_count" ,pages_to_left_count ,";;pages_to_right_count", pages_to_right_count)
 
 
 //         minPage = page - pages_to_left_count;
 //         maxPage = page + pages_to_right_count;
 
 //       }else{
 
 
 //       }
 
       if(totalPages >= SHOW_MAX_PAGES){
 
 
         // check if there are 5 between page and totalPages, else add the diff to before
         // make sure min always starts with 1 irrespective of what prev step says.
 		x = totalPages - page ; // 18 - 2 = 16; (assuming 18 as total and 2 as current page)
 
         if (x >= SHOW_MAX_PAGES){ // 16 > 2
          	 minPage = page;
           	 maxPage = page + SHOW_MAX_PAGES;
 
              // renders  right site pages in pagination
         }else{
 
 
     	  pages_to_right_count = totalPages - page;
           pages_to_left_count = SHOW_MAX_PAGES - pages_to_right_count;
 
 
           minPage = page - pages_to_left_count;
           maxPage = page + pages_to_right_count;
 
 
         }
 
 
       }else{
         // show all the pages
         pages_to_right_count = totalPages - page;
           pages_to_left_count = SHOW_MAX_PAGES - pages_to_right_count;
 
 
           minPage = page - pages_to_left_count;
           maxPage = page + pages_to_right_count;
 
 
       }
       if (minPage <=0 ){
        	minPage = 1;
       }
 
       if (page > 0){
 
 
         if ((page-1) >= 1 && totalPages >= SHOW_MAX_PAGES ){
             $pagination_elems.append('<li class="page-item next "><a href="#" data-page="1" class="page-link"><span class=" fa fa-angle-double-left"></span></a></li>');
 
           $pagination_elems.append('<li class="page-item next"><a href="#" data-page="'+(page-1)+'" class="page-link"><span class="fa fa-angle-left"></span></a></li>');
         }
         for (i=minPage; i <= maxPage; i++){
           if (i == page){
             active = "active"
           }else{
            active = "";
           }
 
          $pagination_elems.append('<li class="page-item '+active+'"><a href="#" data-page="'+i+'" class="page-link">'+i+'</a></li>');
         }
 
         if ( maxPage != totalPages  && totalPages >= SHOW_MAX_PAGES ){
             $pagination_elems.append('<li class="page-item next"><a href="#" data-page="'+(page+1)+'" class="page-link"><span class=" fa fa-angle-right "></span></a></li>');
             $pagination_elems.append('<li class="page-item next "><a href="#" data-page="'+totalPages+'" class="page-link"><span class=" fa fa-angle-double-right"></span></a></li>');
 
         }
       }
 
 //       $pagination_elems.append('<li class="page-item active"><a href="#" class="page-link">1</a></li>');
 
       $pagination.append($pagination_elems);
 
 
       $('.page-link').click(function(){
         	page_num = $(this).attr('data-page');
         	get_page(data, parseInt(page_num), true);
       });
 
       //      <li class="page-item next fa fa-angle-double-left disabled">
 //      <a href="#" class="page-link">&nbsp;</a></li>
 //      <li class="page-item next fa fa-angle-left disabled">
 //      <a href="#" class="page-link">&nbsp;</a></li>
 
 //      <li class="page-item"><a href="#" class="page-link">2</a></li>
 //      <li class="page-item"><a href="#" class="page-link">3</a></li>
 //      <li class="page-item"><a href="#" class="page-link">4</a></li>
 //      <li class="page-item"><a href="#" class="page-link">5</a></li>
 //      <li class="page-item next fa fa-angle-right"><a href="#" class="page-link">&nbsp;</a></li>
 //      <li class="page-item next fa fa-angle-double-right"><a href="#" class="page-link">&nbsp;</a></li>
 
 
 //         var defaultOpts = {
 //             totalPages: totalPages,
 //             currentPage: page,
 //             next: '&nbsp;',
 //             nextClass: 'page-item next fa fa-angle-right',
 //             last: '&nbsp;',
 //             lastClass: 'page-item next fa fa-angle-double-right',
 //             prev: '&nbsp;',
 //             prevClass: 'page-item next fa fa-angle-left',
 //             first: '&nbsp;',

 //             onPageClick: function(event, page) {

     }
 
 
   function find_display_value(result_data, filter_name, filter_value){
     //  if display value exists for this filter_value of filter_name
     // return the display value
     display_value = filter_value;
 
     for (i in result_data.filters){
 
       filter_data = result_data.filters[i];
 
       if (filter_data.name == filter_name){
         for(j in filter_data.values ){
           	filter_unit = filter_data.values[j];
           if (filter_unit.metavalue  == filter_value){
             if (filter_unit.displayvalue ){
               display_value = filter_unit.displayvalue;
             }
 
           }
 
         }
 
       }
 
     }
 
     return display_value;
 
 
   }
 
 
   function generate_applied_filters(data, result_data){
     	$filters_div = $('.relish-search-bar-bottom-filters');
         $filters_div.html("");
         filter_name_map = {}
         for (i  in result_data.filters){
             filter = result_data.filters[i];
             filter_name_map[filter.name] = filter.name;
             if(filter.display_name ){
                 filter_name_map[filter.name]= filter.display_name
             }
         }
 
 
         for (k in data) {
 
             if (k == 'search_query') {
 
             } else if (k == 'q') {
 
             }
           else if (k == 'event_data') {
 
             }
            else if (k == 'uid') {
 
             }
            else if (k == 'event_type') {
 
             }
           else if (k == 'api_token') {
 
             }
               else if (k == 'show_os') {
               }
               else if (k == 'page') {
 
             } else if (k == 'offset') {
 
             } else if (k == 'resultsPerPage') {
 
             } else {
                 if (k == 'sort_method') {
                     $('#relishly-sort-products').val(data[k]);
                 }
                 k_value_data = data[k];
                 k_name = k
                 if (k == "page") {
                 } else {
                     var values = k_value_data.split(','); //seperator
                     for (j in values) {
                         d = {};
                         d[k_name] = values[j]
                         applied_filters.push(d);
 
                         k_name_display = k_name.replace(/_/g, ' ');
                         if (search_string.indexOf("?") > -1) {
                             search_string += "&" + k_name + "=" + values[j];
 
                         } else {
                             search_string += "?" + k_name + "=" + values[j];
                         }
                         if (k_name == "sort_method") {
 
                         } else {
                             data_value = values[j];
                           	// get the display value from the map
                             $filters_div.append('<span>' + filter_name_map[k_name] + ": " + find_display_value(result_data, k_name, data_value) + '<a ' +
                                 'class="filter-delete  fs-option" data-value="' + data_value + '" data-group="' + k_name + '">x</span></a>');
                         }
                     }
                 }
             }
         }
 
 
     	$('.filter-delete').click(function() {
             var filter_name = $(this).attr('data-group');
             var filter_value = $(this).attr('data-value');
             $('.fs-option[data-group="' + filter_name + '"][data-value="' + filter_value + '"]').click();
         });
 
   }
 
     function generate_urlstring(data){
         applied_filters = []
         search_string = window.location.pathname ;
 
         try {
             search_string += "?q=" + data['search_query'];
         } catch (e) {
             search_string += "?q=";
         }
         for (k in data) {
 
             if (k == 'search_query') {
 
             } else if (k == 'q') {
 
             }
           else if (k == 'event_data') {
 
             }
            else if (k == 'uid') {
 
             }
            else if (k == 'event_type') {
 
             }
           else if (k == 'api_token') {
 
             }
            else if (k == 'show_os') {
 
             }else if (k == 'page') {
 
             } else if (k == 'offset') {
 
             } else if (k == 'resultsPerPage') {
 
             } else {
                 if (k == 'sort_method') {
                     $('#relishly-sort-products').val(data[k]);
                 }
                 k_value_data = data[k];
                 k_name = k
                 if (k == "page") {
                 } else {
                     var values = k_value_data.split(',');
                     for (j in values) {
                         d = {};
                         d[k_name] = values[j]
                         applied_filters.push(d);
 
                         k_name_display = k_name.replace(/_/g, ' ');
                         if (search_string.indexOf("?") > -1) {
                             search_string += "&" + k_name + "=" + encodeURIComponent(values[j]);
 
                         } else {
                             search_string += "?" + k_name + "=" + encodeURIComponent(values[j]);
                         }
 
                     }
                 }
             }
         }
 
         search_string += "&page=" + data['page'];
       	return search_string;
     }
     function get_page(data, page, onclicked_call) {
 		/*
         onclicked_call is not used anymore; test thorougly and we can remove it.
         */
         is_mobile = detectmob();
         if (is_mobile) {
             pp = RELISHLY_SEARCH_RESULTS_MOBILE_PP;
         } else {
             pp = RELISHLY_SEARCH_RESULTS_PP;
         }
         data['page'] = page;
 
         $filters_div = $('.relish-search-bar-bottom-filters');
         $filters_div.html("");
       	search_string = generate_urlstring(data);
 
         window.history.replaceState(null, null, search_string);
 
 
 
         data['offset'] = (pp * page) - pp;
         data['resultsPerPage'] = pp;
         data['search_query'] = clean_string(data['search_query']);
 
       	referer_url = window.location.href;
         try{
           keyword = data['search_query'];
           filter_data = data;
           track_search(keyword, filter_data, referer_url)
         }catch(e){
         }
         data['api_token'] = apikey;
 
 
   		$('input[name="q"]').each(function( index ){
         	// get the q = and place
         	$(this).val(decodeURIComponent(data['search_query']));
       	});
 
 
       data['show_os'] = show_os;
 
         $.ajax({
             url: RELISHLY_SEARCH_API,
             data: data,
             dataType: 'json',
             success: function(datas) {
                 if (datas.status) {
                   if (datas.status.indexOf('error') >= 0) {
                     datas = {
                       "products": [],
                       "filters": [],
                       "num_results": 0
                     }
                       render_pagination(0, 0, onclicked_call);
 
                   }
                 }
 
                 if(datas.num_results ){
                   if (datas.num_results == 0) {
 
                     generate_applied_filters({}, {});
 
                       $('#query_count').html("");
 //                                         process_result_data({}, data['search_query'])
 
                       $('.relish-search-results').html("<h3 class='text-muted'>Sorry, no results found. Please try modifying your search.</h3>");
                     render_pagination(0, 0, onclicked_call);
 
                   } else {
 
                       generate_applied_filters(data, datas);
 
                       process_result_data(datas, data['search_query'])
                       $('.relish-search-bar-bottom').show();
                       var low_num = ((page - 1) * (pp));
                       var top_num = (page * pp);
                       if (top_num >= datas.num_results) {
                           var top_num = datas.num_results;
                       }
                       totalPages = Math.ceil(datas.num_results / pp);
                       if (datas.num_results == 0) {
                           $('#query_count').html("");
                       } else {
                           $('#query_count').html("showing " + (low_num + 1) + " - " + top_num + " of " + datas.num_results + "");
                       }
 						// datas is the results data, data is pre ajax data.
                       render_pagination(page, totalPages, onclicked_call);
 
 
                   }
                 } else{
                      $('#query_count').html("");
                       $('.relish-search-results').html("<h3 class='text-muted'>Sorry, no results found. Please try modifying your search.</h3>");
 
                   }
             },
             error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                 datas = {
                     "products": [],
                     "filters": [],
                     "num_results": 0
                 }
                 process_result_data(datas, null )
                 render_pagination({}, 0, onclicked_call);
 
             }
         });
     }
 
     function get_search_results(search_query, page, extra_kwargs) {
         search_query = clean_string(search_query);
         data = {
             'page': page,
             'search_query': search_query,
         }
         // map the url params into a dictionary which can be used when sending the
         // data to the api call in get_page
         for (_k in extra_kwargs) {
             k = extra_kwargs[_k]['key'];
             v = extra_kwargs[_k]['value'];
             if (k in data) {
                 data[k] = clean_string(data[k] + "," + v);
             } else {
                 data[k] = clean_string(v);
             }
         }
         get_page(data, page, false);
     }
 
     function create_products_html(html_list) {
         $products_div = $(RELISHLY_SEARCH_RESULTS);
         for (i in html_list) {
             var product = html_list[i];
             $products_div.append(product);
         }
 
         var currency_ = jQuery('[name=currencies]').val();
 
         try {
             if (jQuery('[name=currencies]').val() == shopCurrency) {
                 Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, jQuery('[name=currencies]').val());
             } else {
                 Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, jQuery('[name=currencies]').val());
             }
         } catch (e) {
 
         }
     }
 
 
 
 
     function create_filters_html(html_list) {
         $filters_div = $(RELISHLY_SEARCH_SIDEBAR);
         $filters_div.html(html_list);
     }
 
       function roundHalf(num) {
         return Math.round(num*2)/2;
     }
 
     function render_rating_star(ratings_count, rating, show_up) {
 
 
 		rating = roundHalf(parseFloat(rating));
 //         rating = parseInt(rating);
 		console.log(rating);
 
       if (Number.isInteger(rating)){
         rating_html = "<i class='fa fa-star' aria-hidden='true'></i>".repeat(rating);
         rating_html += "<i class='fa fa-star-o' aria-hidden='true'></i>".repeat(5 - rating);
 
       }
       else{
 
         var rating_floored = Math.floor(rating);
 
         rating_html = "<i class='fa fa-star' aria-hidden='true'></i>".repeat(rating_floored);
         rating_html += "<i class='fa fa-star-half-o' aria-hidden='true'></i>".repeat(1);
 
         rating_html += "<i class='fa fa-star-o' aria-hidden='true'></i>".repeat(5 - (rating_floored + 1));
 
       }
 
         if (show_up) {
             if (rating <= 4) {
                 rating_html += "<span> & Up </span>";
             }
         }
         if (ratings_count) {
             rating_html += "<span> (" + ratings_count + ")</span>";
 
         }
         return rating_html;
 
     }
 
 
 
     function render_product(product, q) {
         var image = product.image;
         var price = product.price;
         var price = price.toFixed(2).replace(/(\d)(?=(\d{3})+\.)/g, '$1,');
 
       	url_arg = "";
         if (product.variant_id){
           url_arg = "?variant=" +  product.variant_id;
         }
 
       if(url_arg.indexOf("?") > -1 ){
 
         url_arg += '&rly_keyword=' + q + '&rly_referral_type=srp'+ '&rly_pid='+product.id ;
 
       }else{
         url_arg += '?rly_keyword=' + q + '&rly_referral_type=srp'+ '&rly_pid='+product.id ;
 
       }
       if(typeof product.review_rating != 'undefined'){
          var rating = product.review_rating; //  parseInt();
 
         var ratings_count = product.review_count;
         rating_html = render_rating_star(ratings_count, rating)
       }else{
        	rating_html = "";
       }
 
 
 
 
 
       if (product.multiple_variant_prices){
         price_prefix_from = "from";
       }else{
                 price_prefix_from = "";
 
       }
         var $product_item = $('<div class="col-md-4 product-card">' +
             '<a data-click-type="srp" data-keyword="'+ q +'" href="/products/' + product.handle + url_arg +'"><article class="col-item">' +
             '<div class="photo">' +
             '<a data-click-type="srp" data-keyword="'+ q +'" href="/products/' + product.handle + url_arg +'"> <img src="' + image + '" class="img-responsive" alt="Product Image"> </a>' +
             '</div>' +
             '<div class="info">' +
             '<div class="row">' +
             '<div class="price-details col-sm-12">' +
             '<h3><a data-click-type="srp" data-keyword="'+ q +'" href="/products/' + product.handle + url_arg +'">' + product.title + '</a></h3>' +
              price_prefix_from + ' '+ '<span class="money">'  + price + '</span><div class="clearfix"></div>' + rating_html +
             '</div>' +
             '</div>' +
             '</div>' +
             '</article></a></div>');
 
         return $product_item;
     }
 
     function render_filter(data) {
         //var url = new URL(location.href);
         var url_search_string = clean_string(window.location.search); // .search.replace(/%20/g , " ").replace(/%27/g, "'");
 
         if (data.display_name == undefined) {
             display_name = data.name;
 
         } else {
             display_name = data.display_name;
         }
         var filter_name_raw = data.name;
 //         var filter_name = data.name + "::" + display_name; //.replace('_', ' ');
         var filter_values = data.values || [];
 
         is_mobile = detectmob();
         if (is_mobile) {
             show_elems_count = 0;
         } else {
             show_elems_count = 4
         }
 
         $div = $('<div class="filters"></div>');
         less = '<div class="show-more show-more-mobile" > <a href="#" id="filter-more-' + filter_name_raw + '"><i class="fa fa-chevron-down" aria-hidden="true"></i></a></div>';
         if (is_mobile) {
             $div.append($('<div class="product-filter fs-optgroup-label show-more-mobile-dropdown" id="filter-' + filter_name_raw + '" data-group="' + filter_name_raw + '" >' + display_name + less + '</div>'));
         } else {
             $div.append($('<div class="product-filter fs-optgroup-label" id="filter-' + filter_name_raw + '" data-group="' + filter_name_raw + '" >' + display_name + '</div>'));
         }
 
 
 
 
         $.each(filter_values, function(index, data) {
             if (index < show_elems_count) {
                 show_class = "always"
             } else {
                 show_class = "hidden"
             }
             var selected = "";
 
           	//& at the end will help make a extact match even though we are using IndexOf
             if (url_search_string.indexOf(filter_name_raw + "=" + data.metavalue+"&") >= 0) {
                 selected = "selected";
             }
 
             if (filter_name_raw == 'review_rating_range') {
 
                 data_html = render_rating_star(data.count, data.review_rating_image, true)
             } else {
                 data_html = data.displayvalue + '(' + data.count + ')';
             }
             var $html = $('<div class="product-filter product-filter-' + filter_name_raw + ' ' + show_class + ' ' + selected + ' fs-option"' +
                 'data-value="' + data.metavalue + '" data-group="' + filter_name_raw + '"></div>');
             $html.append('<span class="fs-checkbox"><i></i></span>');
             $html.append('<div class="fs-option-label" data-displayvalye="'+data.displayvalue+'" data-value="' + data.metavalue + '">' + data_html + '</div>');
             $div.append($html);
             if (is_mobile) {} else {
                 if (index > show_elems_count + 1) {
                     if (index == filter_values.length - 1) {
                         $div.append($('<div class="show-more" > <a href="#" id="filter-more-' + filter_name_raw + '">Show more</a></div>'));
                     }
                 }
             }
         });
 
 
         return $div;
     }
 
 
 
 
     function start_rendering_search_page(store_name) {
 
 
         q = get_keyword();
         q = clean_string(q);
 
         $('#query_string').html(decodeURIComponent(q));
 
         search_string = window.location.search;
         var search_params = [];
 
         if (search_string.indexOf('&') < 0) {
 
         } else {
             var args = search_string.split("&");
             for (i in args) {
                 if (args[i].indexOf("?") < 0) {
                     var arg_list = args[i].split("=");
                     d = {
                         key: arg_list[0],
                         value: clean_string(arg_list[1])
                     }
                     search_params.push(d);
                 }
             }
         }
 
 
       if (search_string.indexOf('page=') >= 0){
 
           page = search_string.split("page=")[1].split("&")[0]
           page = parseInt(page);
       }else{
           page = 1;
       }
       // check the page
         get_search_results(q, page, search_params);
 
 
 
     }
 
 
     if (is_search_page && is_search_enabled && is_relishly_key_verified) {
 
         // hide the shop data
         // $hide_content.appendTo($('head'));
 
         // 2. get the template from the <script type=text/template"> and show in the page
         var template_data = $('#product-container').html(); // product-container is a
         $(RELISHLY_SEARCH_SANITIZE).html(template_data);
 
         // 3. render the data to the template
         start_rendering_search_page(store_name); // code in relishly-search-js.liquid
 
         $('style#relishly-hide-page-results').remove()
     }
 
 
     $('#relishly-sort-products').change(function() {
 
         var url_params = [];
         var d = {
             'value': $(this).val(),
             'key': 'sort_method',
         }
         url_params.push(d);
         $('.fs-option.selected').each(function(i, el) {
             el = $(el);
             var d = {
                 'value': $(el).find('.fs-option-label').attr('data-value'),
                 'key': $(el).attr('data-group')
             }
             url_params.push(d);
         });
 
         q = get_keyword();
         get_search_results(q, 1, url_params);
 
     });
 
 
   $(document).on("click", ".show-more-mobile-dropdown", function(e){
      var filter_elem = $(this).find('.show-more a')
      var filter_id = $(filter_elem).attr('id').replace('filter-more-', '');
 	 filter_more_id = "filter-more" + filter_id ;
 
 
 
   		if ($(filter_elem).html().indexOf('<i class="fa fa-chevron-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>') != -1) {
             $(filter_elem).html('<i class="fa fa-chevron-up" aria-hidden="true"></i>')
 
             var hidden_els = $('.product-filter-' + filter_id + '.hidden')
             hidden_els.addClass('not-hidden').removeClass('hidden')
 
         } else if ($(filter_elem).html().indexOf('<i class="fa fa-chevron-up" aria-hidden="true"></i>') != -1) {
             $(filter_elem).html('<i class="fa fa-chevron-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>')
             $('.product-filter-' + filter_id + '.not-hidden').addClass('hidden')
 
         };
     	initiate_show_more_listeners();
 
 
   });
 
 
   function initiate_show_more_listeners(){
     // re-initiate this function whenver a .show-more element is dynamically changed
     $(document).on("click", ".show-more a", function(e) {
         e.preventDefault();
 
         var filter_id = $(this).attr('id').replace('filter-more-', '');
 
         if ($(this).text() == "Show more") {
             $(this).text("Show less")
             var hidden_els = $('.product-filter-' + filter_id + '.hidden')
             hidden_els.addClass('not-hidden').removeClass('hidden')
 
         } else if ($(this).text() == "Show less") {
             $(this).text("Show more")
             $('.product-filter-' + filter_id + '.not-hidden').addClass('hidden')
 
         } else if ($(this).html().indexOf('<i class="fa fa-chevron-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>') != -1) {
             $(this).html('<i class="fa fa-chevron-up" aria-hidden="true"></i>')
 
             var hidden_els = $('.product-filter-' + filter_id + '.hidden')
             hidden_els.addClass('not-hidden').removeClass('hidden')
 
         } else if ($(this).html().indexOf('<i class="fa fa-chevron-up" aria-hidden="true"></i>') != -1) {
             $(this).html('<i class="fa fa-chevron-down" aria-hidden="true"></i>')
             $('.product-filter-' + filter_id + '.not-hidden').addClass('hidden')
 
         };
 
 
     });
 
   }
 
 	initiate_show_more_listeners();

 //       console.log("relishly-filters-slide-toggle");
       $(".box").animate({
         width: "toggle"
       });
   });
 
   }

       $(window).load(function() {
     var user_id = $('#insta_user_id').attr('data-id');
     var access_token = $('#insta_access_token').attr('data-token');
     var i, div_lth;
     var ajax_url = 'https://api.instagram.com/v1/users/'+user_id+'/media/recent/?access_token='+access_token;
     
     $.ajax({
       url: ajax_url,
       type: "GET",
       async:false,
       dataType: "jsonp",
       headers: {
         "access-control-allow-origin": true,
         "content-type": "application/json"
       },
       success: function(object){
         div_lth = '';
         console.log(object);
         for(i=0; i<8; i++){
           if(typeof object.data[i] == "undefined"){}
           else{
             div_lth += '<li><figure class="zoom-effect"><a href="'+object.data[i].link+'" target="_blank" id="'+object.data[i].id+'"><img src="'+object.data[i].images.standard_resolution.url+'" alt="instagram" /><span><img src="//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2203/1781/t/2/assets/instagram-icon.png?17332282227607802118">'+object.data[i].likes.count+' likes</span></a></figure></li>';
           }
         }
         $('#instagram_section').append(div_lth);
          setTimeout(function() {
           $('.insta_slider').slick({
             arrows: false,
             infinite: true,
             speed: 1000,
             slide: 'li',
             slidesToShow: 8,
             adaptiveHeight: true,
             autoplay: false,
             dots: false,
             responsive: [
               {
                 breakpoint: 1024,
                 settings: {
                   slidesToShow: 4,
                   slidesToScroll: 1
                 }
               },
               {
                 breakpoint: 769,
                 settings: {
                   slidesToShow: 3,
                   slidesToScroll: 1
                 }
               },
               {
                 breakpoint: 623,
                 settings: {
                   slidesToShow: 2,
                   slidesToScroll: 1
                 }
               },
               {
                 breakpoint: 480,
                 settings: {
                   slidesToShow: 1,
                   slidesToScroll: 1
                 }
               }
 
             ]
           });
 
         },500);
       },
       error: function (xhr, status, error) {
         console.log(status);
         console.log(error);
       }
     });
 
     });

 				} else {
 					script.onload = function() {
 						callback();
 					};
 				}
 				script.src = url;
 				document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
 			};
 			// This is our JavaScript that we'll run after jQuery is included
 			var reChargeThemeFooterJS = function($) {
 				function reChargeSaveCartNoteAndRedirectToCart() {
 					var has_cart_note_or_attribute = false;
 					try {
 						var data = {};
 						if ($('[name="note"]').val() != undefined) {
 							var note = $('[name="note"]').val();
 							data['note'] = note;
 							has_cart_note_or_attribute = true;
 						}
 						if (has_cart_note_or_attribute) {
 							$.ajax({
 								type: 'POST',
 								data: data,
 								url: '/cart/update.js',
 								dataType: 'json',
 								success: function() {
 									window.location.href = '/cart';
 								}
 							});
 						} else {
 							window.location.href = '/cart';
 						}
 					} catch (e) {
 						window.location.href = '/cart';
 					}
 				}
 				var checkout_button_selectors = '[href="/checkout"], form[action="/cart"] button[type="submit"], form[action="/cart"] input[type="submit"], form[action="/checkout"] input[type="submit"], form[action="/checkout"] button[type="submit"]';
 				$(document).on('click', checkout_button_selectors, function(e) {
 					if (!$(this).data('disable-recharge')) {
 						e.preventDefault();
 						reChargeSaveCartNoteAndRedirectToCart();
 						window.location.href = '/cart';
 					}
 				});
 			}
 			// Check if jQuery is added, if not, then we'll loadScript, otherwise, run reChargeJS
 			if ((typeof(jQuery) == 'undefined') || (parseInt(jQuery.fn.jquery) == 1 && parseFloat(jQuery.fn.jquery.replace(/^1\./,"")) < 7.2)) {
 				// We'll get our jQuery from Google APIs
 				loadScript('//ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/1.7.2/jquery.min.js', function() {
 					jQuery172 = jQuery.noConflict(true);
 					reChargeThemeFooterJS(jQuery172);
 				});
 			} else {
 				reChargeThemeFooterJS(jQuery);
 			}
 		})();
   </script>

   <script>
    Currency.format = 'money_with_currency_format';
   var shopCurrency = 'USD';
   /* Sometimes merchants change their shop currency, let's tell our JavaScript file */
   Currency.moneyFormats[shopCurrency].money_with_currency_format = "${{amount}}";
   Currency.moneyFormats[shopCurrency].money_format = "${{amount}}";
 
   /* Default currency */
   var defaultCurrency = 'USD';
 
   /* Cookie currency */
   var cookieCurrency = Currency.cookie.read();
   /* Fix for customer account pages */
   jQuery('span.money span.money').each(function() {
     jQuery(this).parents('span.money').removeClass('money');
   });
   /* Saving the current price */
   jQuery('span.money').each(function() {
     jQuery(this).attr('data-currency-USD', jQuery(this).html());
   });
     // If there's no cookie.
     if (cookieCurrency == null) {
       if (shopCurrency !== defaultCurrency) {
         Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, defaultCurrency);
       }
       else {
         Currency.currentCurrency = defaultCurrency;
       }
     }
     // If the cookie value does not correspond to any value in the currency dropdown.
     else if (jQuery('[name=currencies]').length && jQuery('[name=currencies] option[value=' + cookieCurrency + ']').length === 0) {
       Currency.currentCurrency = shopCurrency;
       Currency.cookie.write(shopCurrency);
     } 
     else if (cookieCurrency === shopCurrency) {
       Currency.currentCurrency = shopCurrency;
     }
     else {
       Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, cookieCurrency);
     }
 
     jQuery('[name=currencies]').val(Currency.currentCurrency).change(function() {
       var newCurrency = jQuery(this).val();
       Currency.convertAll(Currency.currentCurrency, newCurrency);
       jQuery('.selected-currency').text(Currency.currentCurrency);
     });
     var original_selectCallback = window.selectCallback;
     var selectCallback = function(variant, selector) {
       original_selectCallback(variant, selector);
       Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, jQuery('[name=currencies]').val());
       jQuery('.selected-currency').text(Currency.currentCurrency);
     };
     $('body').on('ajaxCart.afterCartLoad', function(cart) {
       Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, jQuery('[name=currencies]').val());
       jQuery('.selected-currency').text(Currency.currentCurrency);  
     });
     jQuery('.selected-currency').text(Currency.currentCurrency);
 
     function currenciesCallbackSpecial(id){
       jQuery(id).each(function() {
         jQuery(this).attr('data-currency-usd', jQuery(this).html());
       });
       Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, Currency.cookie.read(), id);
     }
   </script>
